Note: Find "Node(s) placed on [CPUExecutionProvider]" and "Node(s) placed on [VitisAIExecutionProvider]" to see what operators are used for each EP.
Looks like the VitisAIEP just gets MATMULNBITS partitioned to it, but for some reason the nodes' names are just "vitis_ai_ep_[x]" unlike with the CPU nodes.
